<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="historical">Historical Fantasy</h3>



<p>Historical Fantasy blurs the line between the real and the imagined, weaving magic and the supernatural into the fabric of historical events and settings. </p>



<p>This subgenre takes us on a journey through the annals of time, but with an enchanting twist – history as we know it is infused with fantastical elements, mythical creatures, and magical occurrences. </p>



<p>It&#8217;s a perfect blend for those who love the richness of history and the allure of fantasy.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://www.amazon.com/Babel-Necessity-Violence-Translators-Revolution/dp/0063021439" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/W/MEDIAX_849526-T3/images/I/51V5PZXFdVL._SY445_SX342_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation:</strong> <a href="https://joncronshaw.com/2022/08/25/the-captivating-magic-system-of-r-f-kuangs-babel/" title="The Captivating Magic System of R.F. Kuang’s Babel">&#8220;Babel&#8221; by R. F. Kuang</a> is an exceptional historical fantasy novel for those who appreciate a blend of academic intrigue and magical elements. </p>



<p>Set in the early 19th century, the story unfolds at Oxford University&#8217;s fictional Babel Institute, a centre of translation and linguistic scholarship that harbours a dark secret. </p>



<p>&#8220;Babel&#8221; is particularly recommended for readers who enjoy thought-provoking fantasy with strong ties to real historical events and themes.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://www.amazon.com/Babel-Necessity-Violence-Translators-Revolution/dp/0063021439" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="hopepunk">Hopepunk</h3>



<p>Explore the captivating world of underdogs in fantasy literature, where unlikely heroes from Frodo Baggins to Vin take center stage.</p>



<p>Discover how these relatable characters, with their struggles and triumphs, add depth and resonance to fantasy tales, making them more engaging and inspiring for readers.</p>



<p>Hopepunk is characterized by its focus on optimism, kindness, and the fight for positive change.</p>



<p>It stands in contrast to grimdark fantasy, celebrating characters who combat cynicism and despair through acts of compassion, bravery, and resilience.</p>



<p>Hopepunk stories emphasize the power of hope and community as tools to resist and overcome a harsh and oppressive world.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/rWYVS" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/81nmLYgG1iL._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation:</strong> &#8220;Good Omens&#8221; by Neil Gaiman and Terry Pratchett is an excellent representation of Hopepunk.</p>



<p>This novel, blending humor and fantasy, tells the story of an angel and a demon teaming up to prevent the apocalypse.</p>



<p>It&#8217;s a tale that combines wit, unlikely friendships, and a heartwarming message about the power of human nature to avert disaster, even when the odds seem insurmountable.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://geni.us/rWYVS" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="indian">Indian Fantasy</h3>



<p>Indian Fantasy, while not widely known by a specific name, encompasses fantasy narratives inspired by the diverse myths, legends, and cultural stories of India.</p>



<p>This subgenre often includes elements from Hindu epics, Indian folklore, and historical settings, blending them with magical and fantastical aspects.</p>



<p>Indian Fantasy is rich with diverse characters, intricate plotlines, and themes deeply rooted in Indian philosophy and spirituality.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/Sd7O" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/51vzRJuZ+nL._SY445_SX342_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation:</strong> &#8220;The Devourers&#8221; by Indra Das is a standout Indian Fantasy novel.</p>



<p>It weaves together Indian folklore and history with a compelling narrative about werewolves, shape-shifters, and a journey that spans centuries.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://geni.us/Sd7O" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="isekai">Isekai</h3>



<p>Sekai, a subgenre originating from Japanese literature and media, revolves around a character being transported, reborn, or trapped in an alternate world or parallel universe.</p>



<p>This world often differs significantly from the character’s original reality, often featuring fantasy or sci-fi elements.</p>



<p>The narrative typically focuses on the protagonist&#8217;s adaptation to and exploration of the new world, overcoming challenges, and often fulfilling a particular destiny or quest.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/8ptOuqX" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/81VzX6bu3kL._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation:</strong> &#8220;Sword Art Online&#8221; by Reki Kawahara is a well-known example of Isekai.</p>



<p>It follows the story of players trapped in a virtual MMORPG (Massively Multiplayer Online Role-Playing Game), blending elements of fantasy, adventure, and technology, as they struggle to survive and escape the game.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://geni.us/8ptOuqX" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="legendary">Legendary/Mythic Fantasy</h3>



<p>Legend/Myth Fantasy takes inspiration from the rich tapestry of global myths, legends, and folklore.</p>



<p>This subgenre reinterprets and reimagines these ancient stories, often giving them new life or a fresh perspective.</p>



<p>Whether it&#8217;s through retelling these tales in modern settings or reworking them into new narratives, Legend/Myth Fantasy bridges the gap between the ancient and the contemporary, bringing timeless themes and archetypes into new contexts.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/WsZwt" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/91PUrrAH4QL._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation:</strong> &#8220;American Gods&#8221; by Neil Gaiman is an excellent example.</p>



<p>It brings together deities and mythological beings from various cultures into the modern-day United States, exploring themes of belief, cultural identity, and change.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://geni.us/WsZwt" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="lgbtq">LGBTQ+ Fantasy</h3>



<p>LGBTQ+ Fantasy is a subgenre that features characters and stories that represent the LGBTQ+ community.</p>



<p>These narratives often explore themes of identity, acceptance, and love, set against the backdrop of fantastical worlds.</p>



<p>By including diverse sexual orientations and gender identities, LGBTQ+ Fantasy offers a more inclusive perspective, reflecting the richness of human experience in the realm of fantasy storytelling.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/akFB" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/91JR5HRL84L._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation: </strong>&#8220;The Priory of the Orange Tree&#8221; by Samantha Shannon is an exemplary LGBTQ+ Fantasy novel.</p>



<p>It presents a world rich with dragons, lore, and intrigue, and features a diverse cast of characters, including strong LGBTQ+ representation, interwoven in a tale of conflict, alliance, and romance.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="LitRPG">LitRPG</h3>



<p>LitRPG (Literary Role Playing Game) is a subgenre where the narrative structure and progression follow the mechanics of a role-playing game (RPG).</p>



<p>These stories often feature characters who are aware they are in a game or a game-like world, complete with leveling up, skill acquisition, and other RPG elements.</p>



<p>The genre appeals to readers who enjoy the intersection of gaming and storytelling, offering a detailed exploration of characters&#8217; progression and the gaming world&#8217;s mechanics.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/91tFXY3EnHL._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation:</strong> &#8220;The Land: Founding&#8221; by Aleron Kong is a notable LitRPG novel.</p>



<p>It follows the story of a man transported into a fantastical game world, where he must learn to survive and thrive according to the game&#8217;s rules, balancing action and character development with the intricacies of RPG elements.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://www.amazon.com/Land-Founding-LitRPG-Chaos-Seeds-ebook/dp/B0172GEB68/" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="lost">Lost World</h3>



<p>Lost World Fantasy involves the discovery of unknown and hidden civilizations or worlds, often in unexplored regions like jungles, islands, or underground.</p>



<p>These narratives tap into the allure of exploration and the unknown, featuring elements such as ancient societies, exotic creatures, and forgotten lands.</p>



<p>Lost World stories often combine adventure, mystery, and sometimes speculative elements, exploring the consequences and moral dilemmas of encountering these hidden realms.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/Xq50" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/81YCJbUAXNS._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation:</strong> &#8220;The Lost World&#8221; by Sir Arthur Conan Doyle is a seminal work in this genre.</p>



<p>It tells the story of an expedition to a plateau in the Amazon basin where prehistoric animals still exist, exploring themes of adventure, discovery, and the clash between modern world and ancient realms.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="low">Low Fantasy</h3>



<p>Low Fantasy is characterized by its setting in a realistic world, similar to our own, but with the inclusion of magical or supernatural elements.</p>



<p>Unlike High Fantasy, where the story takes place in a completely different world, Low Fantasy weaves its fantastical aspects into familiar, everyday settings.</p>



<p>This genre often explores the impact of the supernatural on ordinary life and typically features more grounded, relatable characters and scenarios.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/9MAH7i" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/91uu40FbPiL._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation: </strong>&#8220;Pan&#8217;s Labyrinth&#8221; by Guillermo del Toro and Cornelia Funke, based on the film, is an excellent example of Low Fantasy.</p>



<p>Set in post-Civil War Spain, it tells the story of a young girl who encounters a mysterious labyrinth and a faun who sets her on a fantastical quest, blurring the lines between reality and fantasy.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://geni.us/9MAH7i" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="realism">Magical Realism</h3>



<p>Magical Realism is a subgenre where magic is woven into the fabric of the real world, presenting a universe that is almost like our own but with an underlying layer of the extraordinary.</p>



<p>Unlike traditional fantasy, Magical Realism often doesn&#8217;t involve grand battles between good and evil or epic quests.</p>



<p>Instead, it focuses on everyday experiences and relationships, with elements of magic serving to highlight the surreal and extraordinary aspects of ordinary life.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/N655C" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/714ZLzX852L._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation: </strong>&#8220;One Hundred Years of Solitude&#8221; by Gabriel García Márquez, previously mentioned, remains a defining work of Magical Realism.</p>



<p>It tells the multi-generational story of the Buendía family in the fictitious town of Macondo, blending the real with the fantastic in a narrative that reflects the political and cultural realities of Latin America.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="girl">Magical Girl</h3>



<p>The Magical Girl subgenre, originating from Japanese media, revolves around characters, typically young girls or teenagers, who possess magical abilities.</p>



<p>These stories often focus on themes of personal growth, friendship, and the battle against evil forces.</p>



<p>The protagonists typically undergo magical transformations to unlock their powers, often while balancing the challenges of their everyday lives.</p>



<p>The genre is known for its positive messages, vibrant storytelling, and the empowerment of its heroines.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/HIAA" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/91oIfq3BIgL._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation: </strong>&#8220;Cardcaptor Sakura&#8221; by CLAMP is a classic example of the Magical Girl genre.</p>



<p>The manga and its adaptations follow the story of Sakura Kinomoto, a young girl who discovers magical powers and embarks on a quest to retrieve a set of magical cards she accidentally scatters around the world.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://geni.us/HIAA" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="medieval">Medieval Fantasy</h3>



<p>Medieval Fantasy draws inspiration from medieval history and is often set in a world similar to our own Middle Ages.</p>



<p>This subgenre features elements such as knights, castles, feudal systems, and often a blend of historical accuracy with fantastical elements like magic and mythical creatures.</p>



<p>It&#8217;s a genre that captivates those who are fascinated by the medieval era and its romanticized notions of chivalry and adventure.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/51O-Do9S2QL._SY445_SX342_.jpg" alt=""/></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation: </strong>&#8220;<a href="https://joncronshaw.com/2024/02/12/exploring-the-lyrical-world-of-the-kingkiller-chronicle/" title="Exploring the Lyrical World of The Kingkiller Chronicle">The Name of the Wind</a>&#8221; by Patrick Rothfuss, earlier mentioned under Epic Fantasy, also embodies elements of Medieval Fantasy.</p>



<p>It’s set in a richly detailed world reminiscent of the Middle Ages, complete with a unique magic system, bards, and ancient lore.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://geni.us/AulBCDA" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>

<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="meta">Meta-Modern Fantasy</h3>



<p><a href="https://joncronshaw.com/2024/02/10/meta-modern-fantasy-the-new-frontier-in-literary-genres/" title="Meta-Modern Fantasy: The New Frontier in Literary Genres">Meta-Modern Fantasy</a> is a relatively new subgenre that blends elements from various literary genres and often includes a self-reflective or metafictional approach.</p>



<p>These narratives might combine fantasy with science fiction, historical fiction, or other genres, creating a multi-layered story that reflects on its own nature.</p>



<p>Meta-Modern Fantasy often explores themes of reality versus illusion and the nature of storytelling itself.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/bcsvl" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/519ySdAeHGS._SY445_SX342_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation:</strong> &#8220;The City We Became&#8221; by N.K. Jemisin is an example of Meta-Modern Fantasy.</p>



<p>The novel, which blends urban fantasy and elements of metafiction, explores the idea of a living, sentient New York City, personified by five individuals, challenging conventional fantasy narratives.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button">Get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="middle">Middle-Grade Fantasy</h3>



<p>Middle-Grade Fantasy is aimed at children aged around 8 to 12 years and often revolves around themes of adventure, friendship, and self-discovery.</p>



<p>These stories feature protagonists who are similar in age to the target audience, allowing readers to identify with their journeys.</p>



<p>The narratives in Middle-Grade Fantasy are more complex than in Children&#8217;s Fantasy, often exploring conflicts and challenges that mirror the experiences of tweens as they navigate their own path towards adolescence.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/KPLhBU7" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/51xsSvctHcL._SY445_SX342_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation: </strong>&#8220;Percy Jackson &amp; The Olympians&#8221; series by Rick Riordan is an excellent Middle-Grade Fantasy.</p>



<p>It centers on Percy Jackson, a young demigod, and his adventures in a world where Greek mythology intersects with the modern day, combining action, humor, and themes relevant to middle-grade readers.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://geni.us/KPLhBU7" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="military">Military Fantasy</h3>



<p>Military Fantasy is a subgenre where the focus is on military life, strategy, and warfare within a fantasy setting.</p>



<p>These stories often feature detailed depictions of battles, military cultures, and the experiences of soldiers, interwoven with elements of magic and fantastical races.</p>



<p>It appeals to readers who are intrigued by the tactical and strategic aspects of warfare in a world where the rules of combat are expanded by the presence of magic and mythical beings.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/OhZN" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/71AymSzADvL._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation:</strong> &#8220;The Black Company&#8221; series by Glen Cook is a seminal work in Military Fantasy.</p>



<p>It tells the story of an elite mercenary unit in a gritty, morally complex world, combining the harsh realities of war with dark and compelling magic.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://geni.us/OhZN" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="mythpunk">Mythpunk</h3>



<p><br>Mythpunk refers to a subgenre that takes traditional myths, folklore, and fairy tales and gives them a new, often subversive twist.</p>



<p>These stories reimagine the familiar narratives, infusing them with modern themes, unconventional storytelling methods, and a punk ethos.</p>



<p>Mythpunk challenges the traditional norms and roles found in ancient myths, offering fresh, sometimes radical perspectives on the stories we thought we knew.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/9z0ZA0" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/81aKum4SnrL._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation: </strong>&#8220;Deathless&#8221; by Catherynne M. Valente is an embodiment of Mythpunk.</p>



<p>The novel reinterprets the Russian folktale of Koschei the Deathless, blending it with historical events like the Russian Revolution and World War II, creating a rich, lyrical, and evocative narrative.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://geni.us/9z0ZA0" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="native">Native American Fantasy</h3>



<p>Native American Fantasy incorporates elements of Native American myths, legends, and folklore into fantasy narratives.</p>



<p>This genre often explores themes central to Native American cultures, such as a deep connection to the land, spirituality, and the impact of colonialism.</p>



<p>These stories can offer a blend of historical and contemporary settings, presenting a unique perspective on Native American life and mythology.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/E2Z9m" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/91gTyTpTvCL._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation:</strong> &#8220;Trail of Lightning&#8221; by Rebecca Roanhorse is a notable example of Native American Fantasy.</p>



<p>The novel is set in a post-apocalyptic world that draws heavily on Navajo mythology, featuring a monster-slaying protagonist navigating a landscape filled with gods and mythological beings.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://geni.us/E2Z9m" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="nautical">Nautical Fantasy</h3>



<p>Nautical Fantasy is a subgenre that combines elements of fantasy with maritime adventures.</p>



<p>These tales are set on the high seas and often feature sailors, pirates, sea monsters, and enchanted islands.</p>



<p>Magic and the supernatural are intertwined with the exploration and adventure of seafaring life.</p>



<p>It’s a genre that captivates with its blend of oceanic lore, swashbuckling action, and fantastical elements, appealing to those who long for tales of the deep and the mysteries it holds.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/lFqBhx2" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/910gyyCG7pL._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation:</strong> &#8220;Liveship Traders&#8221; trilogy by Robin Hobb is an excellent example of Nautical Fantasy.</p>



<p>Set in a richly detailed world of trading ships and pirate seas, it tells the story of sentient ships, sea serpents, and complex characters, weaving a tale of magic, commerce, and maritime adventure.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="new">New Weird</h3>



<p>New Weird is a subgenre that blends elements of fantasy, horror, and science fiction to create stories that defy conventional genre boundaries.</p>



<p>Characterized by surreal worlds, bizarre creatures, and complex narratives, New Weird pushes the limits of imagination, often challenging the reader&#8217;s perceptions of reality.</p>



<p>It&#8217;s a genre for those who revel in the unconventional and seek narratives that are unafraid to explore the strange and the uncanny.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/6EE6yA" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/41nwjrUcklL._SY445_SX342_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation:</strong> &#8220;Perdido Street Station&#8221; by China Miéville is a prime example of New Weird.</p>



<p>Set in the sprawling, chaotic city of New Crobuzon, it weaves a tale rich with strange beings, arcane sciences, and a pervasive sense of wonder and horror.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://geni.us/6EE6yA" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="noblebright">Noblebright Fantasy</h3>



<p>Noblebright Fantasy is characterized by its focus on the themes of hope, courage, and the inherent goodness of people.</p>



<p>In these stories, characters strive to do the right thing and make a positive difference in their world.</p>



<p>It’s a counterpoint to Grimdark Fantasy, emphasizing optimism and the possibility of positive change.</p>



<p><a href="https://joncronshaw.com/2023/07/04/what-is-noblebright-fantasy-a-beginners-guide/" title="What is Noblebright Fantasy? A Beginner’s Guide">Noblebright Fantasy</a> appeals to readers who are looking for uplifting stories where heroes fight against the odds for a cause greater than themselves.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/c11v" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/61XxDdojt1L._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation: </strong>&#8220;The Deed of Paksenarrion&#8221; by Elizabeth Moon is a notable Noblebright Fantasy.</p>



<p>Following the journey of Paksenarrion, a sheepfarmer&#8217;s daughter who dreams of being a hero, it’s a tale of honor, bravery, and the struggle for goodness in a world of conflict and danger.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://geni.us/c11v" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="nobledark">Nobledark Fantasy</h3>



<p>Nobledark Fantasy is a subgenre characterized by its dark, often grim settings, where characters are deeply flawed yet follow a strong moral compass.</p>



<p>In these stories, the world may be bleak or corrupt, but the protagonists strive to uphold their principles and make positive changes, despite the odds and their personal struggles.</p>



<p>It&#8217;s a genre that delves into the complexities of morality and integrity in a world that often seems devoid of both.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/d7PnBb" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/810Mglx1DfL._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation: </strong>The &#8220;<a href="https://joncronshaw.com/2023/08/08/how-robin-hobbs-farseer-trilogy-changed-the-fantasy-genre/" title="How Robin Hobb’s Farseer Trilogy Changed the Fantasy Genre">Farseer Trilogy&#8221; by Robin Hobb</a>, as mentioned, is a quintessential example of Nobledark Fantasy.</p>



<p>Following the life of FitzChivalry Farseer, a royal bastard and assassin in a kingdom fraught with intrigue and danger, the series explores themes of loyalty, sacrifice, and the weight of a moral code in a harsh world.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://geni.us/d7PnBb" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>

</div></figure>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="noir">Noir Fantasy</h3>



<p>Noir Fantasy is a subgenre that blends the gritty, morally ambiguous characteristics of noir fiction with elements of fantasy.</p>



<p>These stories typically feature hard-boiled detectives, shadowy urban settings, and complex plots involving crime and mystery.</p>



<p>The narratives are often characterized by their cynical tone, morally grey characters, and a focus on the darker aspects of society, all set within a fantastical world.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/vq74X" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/A1TKnmVQwRL._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation: </strong>The &#8220;<a href="https://joncronshaw.com/2024/02/17/exploring-stephen-brusts-vlad-taltos-series-a-unique-fantasy-saga/" title="Exploring Stephen Brust’s ‘Vlad Taltos’ Series: A Unique Fantasy Saga">Vlad Taltos&#8221; series by Steven Brust</a>, especially the novel &#8220;Jhereg,&#8221; is an excellent example of Noir Fantasy.</p>



<p>It follows Vlad Taltos, a human assassin in a world dominated by the Dragaeran Empire, combining elements of crime, espionage, and magic in a setting that blends classic noir with high fantasy.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://geni.us/vq74X" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="norse">Norse Fantasy</h3>



<p>Norse Fantasy is a subgenre that draws heavily from <a href="https://joncronshaw.com/2024/01/13/from-horned-helmets-to-yggdrasil-identifying-a-norse-fantasy-world/" title="From Horned Helmets to Yggdrasil: Identifying a Norse Fantasy World">Norse mythology</a>, Viking history, and Scandinavian folklore.</p>



<p>These stories often feature gods, giants, and legendary heroes, set against the backdrop of the rugged Nordic landscape.</p>



<p>Themes commonly explored in Norse Fantasy include fate, heroism, and the struggle against the supernatural, often intertwined with the gritty and adventurous spirit of Viking culture.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/Pdv2iMb" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/91mrguQzr6L._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation:</strong> &#8220;The Hammer and the Cross&#8221; series by Harry Harrison and John Holm is an excellent example of Norse Fantasy.</p>



<p>The novels combine historical elements of the Viking era with Norse mythology, creating a richly detailed and immersive world.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>

<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="paranormal">Paranormal Fantasy</h3>



<p>Paranormal Fantasy blends elements of the fantastical with the modern world, featuring supernatural beings such as vampires, werewolves, witches, and ghosts.</p>



<p>Set in contemporary settings, these narratives often explore the interaction between the supernatural and the mundane, bringing an element of the uncanny into everyday life.</p>



<p>It’s a genre that captivates those intrigued by the idea of hidden worlds and unexplained phenomena existing alongside the familiar.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/ixyO" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/81EXoCsuYyL._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation: </strong>&#8220;The Dresden Files&#8221; by Jim Butcher is an excellent entry into Paranormal Fantasy.</p>



<p>Centering on Harry Dresden, a wizard and private investigator in modern-day Chicago, the series weaves together mystery, magic, and the supernatural in an urban setting.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading">Paranormal Romance (PNR)</h3>



<p>Paranormal Romance is a subgenre where romance is central to the plot and is intertwined with elements of the paranormal or supernatural.</p>



<p>These narratives often feature relationships between humans and supernatural beings like vampires, werewolves, witches, or ghosts.</p>



<p>The stories explore themes of forbidden love, the complexities of relationships between different beings, and the challenges of love in a world where the supernatural is real.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/K79Q2" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/71Iu4NDoePL._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation: </strong>&#8220;Twilight&#8221; series by Stephenie Meyer is a well-known example of Paranormal Romance.</p>



<p>It explores the romantic relationship between a human teenager and a vampire, delving into themes of love, desire, and the supernatural.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://geni.us/K79Q2" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="political">Political Fantasy</h3>



<p>Political Fantasy focuses on the drama and intrigue of political power within a fantasy setting.</p>



<p>These stories are driven by the machinations, alliances, betrayals, and strategic maneuverings of individuals or factions vying for power.</p>



<p>Rather than centering on physical battles or quests, Political Fantasy delves into the psychological and tactical aspects of governance and power struggles, often against a backdrop of a richly built fantasy world.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/YAWw3Zc" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/91lGfuja+5L._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation: </strong>&#8220;The Goblin Emperor&#8221; by Katherine Addison offers an intriguing foray into Political Fantasy.</p>



<p>The novel tells the story of Maia, a half-goblin, half-elf who unexpectedly ascends to the throne of an elven kingdom.</p>



<p>It&#8217;s a tale of court intrigue, diplomacy, and the complexities of ruling in a world filled with prejudice, plots, and power struggles.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://geni.us/YAWw3Zc" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="portal">Portal Fantasy</h3>



<p>Portal Fantasy is a subgenre where characters travel from the real world to a fantastical realm, often through a magical doorway or portal.</p>



<p>These narratives typically focus on the protagonist&#8217;s journey and adaptation to the new world, which is filled with wonder, danger, and often, a quest or mission.</p>



<p>It&#8217;s a genre that captivates with the allure of discovery and the contrast between the familiar and the fantastical.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/TIAJEC1" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/41HKZpU5DxL._SY445_SX342_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation: </strong>&#8220;The Lion, the Witch and the Wardrobe&#8221; by C.S. Lewis is a classic example of Portal Fantasy.</p>



<p>It follows the Pevensie siblings as they step through a wardrobe into the magical land of Narnia, embarking on a journey filled with wonder and adventure.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://geni.us/TIAJEC1" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="post">Post-Apocalyptic Fantasy</h3>



<p>Post-Apocalyptic Fantasy is set in a world that has suffered a catastrophic event, often with magical or supernatural causes.</p>



<p>This subgenre explores themes of survival, the rebuilding of society, and the human spirit&#8217;s resilience in the aftermath of a world-altering calamity.</p>



<p>It combines the ruins of a collapsed civilization with fantastical elements, creating a backdrop for stories of endurance, hope, and rebirth.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/NmGzV" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/915orvpMXZL._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation:</strong> &#8220;The Fifth Season&#8221; by N.K. Jemisin, part of the &#8220;Broken Earth&#8221; trilogy, exemplifies this subgenre.</p>



<p>It portrays a world frequently ravaged by cataclysmic events, where certain individuals wield the power to control geological forces, weaving together themes of apocalypse, magic, and societal upheaval.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://geni.us/NmGzV" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="progression">Progression Fantasy</h3>



<p>Progression Fantasy is a subgenre where the main focus is on the protagonist&#8217;s growth in power and skill over time.</p>



<p>These stories often include detailed systems for magic or power, with characters progressively unlocking new abilities or levels of strength.</p>



<p>The narrative satisfaction comes from following the character’s journey from relative weakness to significant power, often through training, learning, or overcoming challenges.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/ZCDp" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/81Tbf79ePML._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation: </strong>&#8220;Cradle&#8221; series by Will Wight is a notable example of Progression Fantasy.</p>



<p>The series follows the story of Lindon, a young man from a low-powered clan, as he embarks on a journey to become more powerful, featuring a well-defined system of progression and magical martial arts.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link has-text-align-center wp-element-button">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="pulp">Pulp Fantasy</h3>



<p>Pulp Fantasy harks back to the style of the pulp magazines of the early 20th century.</p>



<p>These stories are characterized by their fast pace, sensationalist action, and vivid, sometimes lurid, storytelling.</p>



<p>Pulp Fantasy often features exotic locations, daring heroes, and over-the-top villains.</p>



<p>It’s a genre for those who revel in action-packed adventures and fantastical escapades that prioritize entertainment and escapism.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/YIc4AX" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/71OmDY2KpxL._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation: </strong>&#8220;Conan the Barbarian&#8221; by Robert E. Howard is a quintessential Pulp Fantasy.</p>



<p>Conan’s adventures, set in the mythical Hyborian Age, are replete with sword fights, sorcery, and thrilling exploits, embodying the spirit of pulp fiction.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://geni.us/YIc4AX" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="quest">Quest Fantasy</h3>



<p>Quest Fantasy is a subgenre centered around a central quest or mission.</p>



<p>These stories typically involve a hero or group of heroes embarking on a journey to achieve a specific goal, whether it&#8217;s to retrieve a magical object, save a kingdom, or defeat a formidable villain.</p>



<p>Along the way, they face various challenges and obstacles, both external and internal.</p>



<p>Quest Fantasy is characterized by its narrative structure and the development of its characters through their adventures.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/UTrz" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/418jD+Rsd5L._SY445_SX342_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation:</strong> &#8220;<a href="https://joncronshaw.com/2024/02/07/the-hobbit-paving-the-way-for-modern-fantasy/" title="The Hobbit: Paving the Way for Modern Fantasy">The Hobbit&#8221; by J.R.R. Tolkien</a> is a quintessential Quest Fantasy.</p>



<p>It narrates the journey of Bilbo Baggins, a reluctant hero who joins a group of dwarves on a quest to reclaim their homeland from the dragon Smaug, encountering numerous challenges and transformative experiences along the way.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://geni.us/UTrz" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="roguish">Roguish Fantasy</h3>



<p>Roguish Fantasy centers around characters who are typically on the fringes of society, such as thieves, assassins, or con artists.</p>



<p>These protagonists are often antiheroes or morally grey characters, using their wits, charm, and skills to navigate a world that is not black-and-white in terms of morality.</p>



<p>The stories in this subgenre are filled with intrigue, heists, and clever deceptions, appealing to those who enjoy a more nuanced take on the traditional hero&#8217;s journey.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/x1b4U" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/91pbvnDj5FL._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation: </strong>&#8220;The Lies of Locke Lamora&#8221; by Scott Lynch is an exemplary work in Roguish Fantasy.</p>



<p>It tells the story of Locke Lamora, a master thief, and his band of con artists, weaving a tale of high-stakes heists, complex characters, and a richly imagined world.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-full"><a href="https://geni.us/dawnbox" rel="noopener"><img data-recalc-dims="1" loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="456" height="600" data-attachment-id="6202" data-permalink="https://joncronshaw.com/2023/10/24/assassin-archetypes-the-different-types-of-assassins-youll-encounter-in-fantasy-novels/dawn-box-sm/" data-orig-file="https://i0.wp.com/joncronshaw.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Dawn-box-sm.jpg?fit=456%2C600&amp;ssl=1" data-orig-size="456,600" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;1&quot;}" data-image-title="Dawn-box-sm" data-image-description="" data-image-caption="" data-medium-file="https://i0.wp.com/joncronshaw.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Dawn-box-sm.jpg?fit=228%2C300&amp;ssl=1" data-large-file="https://i0.wp.com/joncronshaw.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Dawn-box-sm.jpg?fit=456%2C600&amp;ssl=1" src="https://i0.wp.com/joncronshaw.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Dawn-box-sm.jpg?resize=456%2C600&#038;ssl=1" alt="" class="wp-image-6202" srcset="https://i0.wp.com/joncronshaw.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Dawn-box-sm.jpg?w=456&amp;ssl=1 456w, https://i0.wp.com/joncronshaw.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Dawn-box-sm.jpg?resize=228%2C300&amp;ssl=1 228w, https://i0.wp.com/joncronshaw.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Dawn-box-sm.jpg?resize=266%2C350&amp;ssl=1 266w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 456px) 85vw, 456px" /></a></figure>
</div>


<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="romantic">Romantic Fantasy</h3>



<p>Romantic Fantasy is a subgenre where romance plays a significant, yet not central, role within a broader fantasy narrative.</p>



<p>In these stories, the romantic subplot is woven into the fabric of the main plot, enriching the overall story without overshadowing the fantasy elements.</p>



<p>Characters may experience love and relationships, but these elements complement the larger themes and adventures of the fantasy world.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/gLOjRrs" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/516QinyJ1CL._SY445_SX342_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation:</strong> &#8220;Uprooted&#8221; by Naomi Novik is an excellent example of Romantic Fantasy.</p>



<p>Set in a world inspired by Eastern European folklore, it tells the story of a young woman who becomes entangled with a mysterious wizard and a malevolent forest, with a beautifully developed romantic subplot enhancing the tale.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="silkpunk">Silkpunk</h3>



<p>Silkpunk is a subgenre that blends elements of Asian culture and history with advanced technology and futuristic concepts, similar to how Steampunk combines Victorian-era aesthetics with steam-powered technology.</p>



<p>Silkpunk stories are often set in fantastical versions of ancient China or other parts of Asia, featuring intricate, silk-inspired designs, advanced engineering, and a deep integration of Asian philosophy and art.</p>



<p>This genre presents a unique fusion of the ancient and the futuristic, showcasing a world where traditional Eastern aesthetics meet cutting-edge innovation.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/1r4Bm" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/81A4MmSRwiL._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation: </strong>&#8220;The Grace of Kings&#8221; by Ken Liu is a prime example of Silkpunk.</p>



<p>The novel weaves a tapestry of rebellion, intrigue, and epic battles in a setting inspired by historical Asia, complete with inventive technologies and mythical creatures.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading" id="slipstream">Slipstream</h3>



<p>Slipstream blurs the boundaries between genres, often merging elements of fantasy, science fiction, and literary fiction.</p>



<p>Characterized by its surreal and dream-like qualities, Slipstream challenges readers&#8217; perceptions of reality and fiction.</p>



<p>It typically eschews conventional narrative structures, instead focusing on the mood and emotional resonance of the story.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/2wV7WJ" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/61zkNbchZ6L._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation: </strong>&#8220;Kafka on the Shore&#8221; by Haruki Murakami is a notable example of Slipstream.</p>



<p>The novel intertwines the seemingly ordinary with the bizarre and metaphysical, weaving a tale that defies easy categorization and immerses readers in a surreal experience.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://geni.us/2wV7WJ" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading">Science Fantasy</h3>



<p>Science Fantasy is a subgenre that blends elements of science fiction, particularly space exploration and futuristic technology, with traditional fantasy themes and motifs.</p>



<p>These narratives often take place in outer space or on other planets, featuring advanced technologies alongside magic, mythical beings, and ancient prophecies.</p>



<p>It’s a genre that appeals to those who dream of a universe where the boundaries between science and magic blur.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/sDr6" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/51QrCdOLPGS._SY445_SX342_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p id="science"><strong>Book Recommendation: </strong>&#8220;Star Wars&#8221; novels, set in the iconic &#8220;Star Wars&#8221; universe, are classic examples of Science Fantasy.</p>



<p>They combine elements of space opera with mystical forces like the Force, intergalactic politics, and epic battles between good and evil.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://geni.us/sDr6" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="sf">Science Fiction (Sci-Fi)</h2>



<p>Science fiction, often abbreviated as sci-fi, explores imaginative concepts primarily influenced by scientific discoveries, space exploration, time travel, parallel universes, and futuristic technology.</p>



<p>This genre often questions the potential consequences of scientific and other innovations, and has been called a &#8220;literature of ideas.&#8221; </p>



<p>Sci-fi typically deals with imaginative and futuristic concepts, such as advanced science and technology, space exploration, time travel, parallel universes, and extraterrestrial life.</p>



<p>Science fiction opens the mind to the endless possibilities of the future, challenging our understanding of science, ethics, and the universe.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/dGLdPS4" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/611vANh0NbL._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation: </strong>&#8220;I, Robot&#8221; by Isaac Asimov is a seminal work in the science fiction genre.</p>



<p>The book, a collection of interconnected short stories, delves into the complexities and ethics of artificial intelligence and robotics. </p>



<p>Asimov&#8217;s introduction of the Three Laws of Robotics and his exploration of their implications make &#8220;I, Robot&#8221; a thought-provoking and foundational text for sci-fi enthusiasts.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>



<p class="has-text-align-right"><a href="#contents" title="">Return to contents &gt;&gt;&gt;</a></p>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading">Steampunk</h3>



<p id="steampunk">Steampunk is characterized by its setting in an alternate history, typically the Victorian era or a similarly industrialized period, where steam-powered technology reigns supreme.</p>



<p>This subgenre incorporates elements of fantasy within a retrofuturistic world, featuring airships, steam engines, and clockwork devices, often combined with magic and adventure.</p>



<p>Steampunk captures the imagination with its unique aesthetic, blending historical settings with imaginative technology and fantastical elements.</p>


<div class="wp-block-image">
<figure class="aligncenter size-large"><a href="https://geni.us/GQS4y1T" rel="noopener"><img decoding="async" src="https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/911EmvM8maL._SY522_.jpg" alt=""/></a></figure>
</div>


<p><strong>Book Recommendation:</strong> &#8220;The Watchmaker of Filigree Street&#8221; by Natasha Pulley offers a compelling foray into the steampunk genre.</p>



<p>Set in Victorian London, the story revolves around a mysterious watchmaker who possesses extraordinary talents. The narrative intertwines elegant clockwork inventions with a thrilling plot, creating an enchanting vision of a steampunk-infused world.</p>



<div class="wp-block-buttons is-content-justification-center is-layout-flex wp-container-core-buttons-is-layout-16018d1d wp-block-buttons-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-button"><a class="wp-block-button__link wp-element-button" href="https://geni.us/GQS4y1T" rel="noopener">get your copy.</a></div>
</div>
